  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_cc104398-6210-45ee-96e0-b114582ca777'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

<div class='answererUserIcon'>
<a class="leftAlignedImage userPhoto" href="/user/show/32017081-victoria"><img alt="" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/users/1401986806i/32017081._UY100_CR25,0,100,100_.jpg" /></a>

<div class='communityAnswerTextContainer'>
<span class='communityAnswererName'>
<a href="/user/show/32017081-victoria">Victoria</a>
</span>
<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">I don't think I would recommend this book to anyone younger than 15-16. Not that I'm naive enough to think that kids younger than that aren't exposed <a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">I don't think I would recommend this book to anyone younger than 15-16. Not that I'm naive enough to think that kids younger than that aren't exposed to sex, drugs, and alcohol in real life, but I simply couldn't in good conscience put this book into the hands of someone younger than that due to the mature themes it contains. Children and teenagers these days are exposed to too much too soon, and I while we can't stop that from happening, we don't have to help it along. Just my two cents. :)<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>
</div>
</div>

<div id="review_301777977" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/301777977" />
    <a title="Anzu The Great Destroyer" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2278800-anzu-the-great-destroyer"><img alt="Anzu The Great Destroyer" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1455829739p2/2278800.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/301777977?book_show_action=true">Mar 27, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Anzu The Great Destroyer" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Anzu The Great Destroyer" href="/user/show/2278800-anzu-the-great-destroyer">Anzu The Great Destroyer</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/13097220-sweet-evil">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">whiny teenage girls</span></div>

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Anzu by: </span>
      someone who wanted to cause me a slow and horrible death
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2278800-anzu-the-great-destroyer?shelf=dat-cover-goddammit">dat-cover-goddammit</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2278800-anzu-the-great-destroyer?shelf=romance-paranormal">romance-paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2278800-anzu-the-great-destroyer?shelf=ya-is-dead">ya-is-dead</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2278800-anzu-the-great-destroyer?shelf=yep-it-was-the-cover">yep-it-was-the-cover</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2278800-anzu-the-great-destroyer?shelf=big-fucking-nope">big-fucking-nope</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2278800-anzu-the-great-destroyer?shelf=facepalm">facepalm</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2278800-anzu-the-great-destroyer?shelf=i-deserved-it">i-deserved-it</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2278800-anzu-the-great-destroyer?shelf=stabby-stabby">stabby-stabby</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2278800-anzu-the-great-destroyer?shelf=nope">nope</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2278800-anzu-the-great-destroyer?shelf=the-hate-it-burns">the-hate-it-burns</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer301777977" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2187264620290126056">I walked right into this one. I admit it and I know it’s my fault, and I probably deserve what I got. However, that doesn’t mean it makes it less painful.<br/><br/><i>Sweet Evil</i> is the most idiotic book I’ve read this year. And I mean it. I totally mean it. I could tell I was going to regret getting it since page one.<br/><blockquote>
  <b>Running had become my new pastime five weeks ago, after I’d read how my body is the “temple of my soul.” Healthy temple: check.</b>
</blockquote><br/>Wha??<br/><br/>Ok, it’s not THAT bad but I still had a feeling deep down </span>
  <span id="freeText2187264620290126056" style="display:none">I walked right into this one. I admit it and I know it’s my fault, and I probably deserve what I got. However, that doesn’t mean it makes it less painful.<br><br><i>Sweet Evil</i> is the most idiotic book I’ve read this year. And I mean it. I totally mean it. I could tell I was going to regret getting it since page one.<br><blockquote>
  <b>Running had become my new pastime five weeks ago, after I’d read how my body is the “temple of my soul.” Healthy temple: check.</b>
</blockquote><br>Wha??<br><br>Ok, it’s not THAT bad but I still had a feeling deep down my heart. It was telling me <i>”Put the book down and walk away.”</i> As you can tell I chose to ignore it.<br><br>Aaanyways, lemme tell you what <i>Sweet Evil</i> is all about. So we have this girl Anna. She is goodness personified. An angel. The perfect girl, pure, sweet hearted, kind, shy, invisible, smart, always does her homework, reminds the teacher that she forgot to check the class’ homework, fucking retarded twit. Yes, she is retarded because I sure can’t figure out how a person can behave the way she does. Higgins wanted to create the perfect sweet little heroine. She failed miserably. Why? Because she made her <b>too perfect</b> to the point that she is not perfect AT ALL. Am I making sense?<br><br>And yes she does see herself ugly but in reality she is so hot that all the boys from their school want to bang her.<br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380373466i/727084.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So we have Saint Anna who is a misunderstood little hipster. She has her Bella Swan mood going on, she’s anti-partying, anti-drinking, anti-drugs (even though she practically drools over alcohol and drugs – but that’s her little secret, shhhh), whatever <i>evil</i> thing you may imagine – she’s against it. Did I mention she’s a virgin?<br><br>But oh no, she’s far from perfect. I mean she has a freckle!!! At the end of her upper lip!!! And people STARE at it when she talks!!! Ugh eeewww that’s so disgusting!!!!<br><br>Oh yes, this makes her a more believable character. SHE HAS FLAWS!!! <br><blockquote>
  <b>“They only think they like me because they don’t know me,” I said.</b>
</blockquote><br>They don’t know me, no one knows me cuz I’m all deep and stuff. <br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380373466i/727084.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Yeah, so Saint Anna is a special kind of bird. She has this mood-ring thing going on. You remember those little things? The mood rings? You put it on and it changes color. And you look at a little chart that tells you what that color says about your current mood. It’s actually a fun thing even though it doesn’t really work. I wish it did though. Anyhow, Anna is a big flat chested mood ring. She sees people’s emotions through the colors they are emitting. And she has a superhero olfactory sense.<br><blockquote>
  <b>Being able to hear and see and smell everything within a one-mile radius was major sensory overload.</b>
</blockquote><br>Then can you sense how overly stinky this book is? Can you Saint Anna???<br><br>All is normal and boring in Saint Anna’s life until she goes at a concert and lays her innocent eyes on a devilish drummer. This vile creature breaks the poor girl’s circuits and turns her into a vixen. Oh my!<br><blockquote>
  <b>“That guy, the drummer? Get this. He’s a killer musician, he gets tons of chicks, his dad’s loaded, and as if that wasn’t enough, he’s got a friggin’ English accent!”</b>
</blockquote><br>Yep, another mysterious handsome rich British-accented teenager. Very original if I do say so myself.<br><br>Why do they all have British accents again? Because they’re smexy? And the funny thing is that mostly American authors feel the need to specify that the hottie has a British accent. That adds to their sexiness. I agree that the accent is special but I’m not falling for it anymore because the idea is being overused. Not fun anymore people so <b>move on</b>!<br><br>So this dude Kaidan, as you can already tell, is another perfect being. Everyone seems to be perfect in this book. Except for her mum, but I’ll get back to that later. So he seems perfect from every way. Wrong. He is actually a stuck up asshole. A big fat loser. And har-di-har-har he’s a demon that feeds on sex.<br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380373466ra/727085.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I’ve read many books where demons were actually behaving like the mischievous creatures that they are. They don’t even compare to this guy. <b>Teenage visions of hotties. You suck.</b> Except for <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8490112.Daughter_of_Smoke_and_Bone__Daughter_of_Smoke_and_Bone___1_" title="Daughter of Smoke and Bone (Daughter of Smoke and Bone, #1) by Laini Taylor" rel="nofollow noopener">Daughter of Smoke and Bone</a>’s Akiva. He’s a piece of art.<br><blockquote>
  <b>[about his name] Kai, like Thai, only yummier. Gah! Who was this girl invading my brain?</b>
</blockquote><br>No, I’m pretty sure that’s the real you. <b>A fucking idiot.</b><br><blockquote>
  <b>Good gracious, he was sexy—a word that had not existed in my personal vocabulary until that moment.</b>
</blockquote><br>Right? It makes you wonder how Higgins sees teenagers, does it not.<br><br><b>The purity!! It BUUUUUUUUURNS!!!</b><br><blockquote>
  <b>I tried to focus on his words and not his luxuriously accented voice, which made everything sound lovely.</b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380373466i/727084.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>Gosh, his eyes were gorgeous—the color of tropical honeymoon waters ringed in dark sapphire and enclosed by thick lashes.</b>
</blockquote><br>Tropical honeymoon waters you say. Honeymoon. Sex. She’s such a vixen right now.<br><br>Oh and by the way he is special too. I forgot to mention this earlier. He has the same mood-ring color bullshit going on as our sweet little Saint Anna. Or at least something similar to that. Useless details that I don’t give a shit about.<br><br>Back to the story. So Kaidan is probably there (I’m not 100% sure about this since I dropped the book around 40% of the way) to guide her towards their people, since they have the same traits and all.<br><br><i>Predictability dangerously close to 80%.</i><br><blockquote>
  <b>“Then what am I?” I asked with apprehension. <br>“Your parents were angels.”</b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380373466ra/727086.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Oh, you’re not joking about that? You’re actually serious?<br><br>Why am I not surprised? Why oh why dear heavens?<br><br><i>DANGER! Predictability has reached 100%. Prepare to abort mission.</i><br><br>And the thing is Patti (her mum) knows about Kaidan being a sexual deviant. She’s not her real mum though, our dearest virgin is adopted. But first thing first, a short introduction for Saint Anna’s mum. <br><br><b>OVERPROTECTIVE</b><br><br>/end of introduction<br><br>So Saint Anna wants to go meet her real dad who is a bad angel of sorts in order to bla bla bla nothing important. And her mum’s too busy to take a day off (???) so she sends her virgin daughter with Kaidan. On a road trip. The two teenagers alone. For a couple of days. And she comes up with the idea herself.<br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380373466ra/727087.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>You’re sending your daughter with a demon and you think she’ll be safe. You go crazy over a party that Saint Anna wanted to attend. You called the parents to make sure the kids will be supervised and all. We wouldn’t want some random jock choke on a glass of beer now, would we? And now the Virgin Anna wants to go out of town with the hottest dude on the planet that happens to be a demon. And you’re ok with it.<br><br>That’s great parenting Patti, you should write a book about it.<br><br>Eventually they go on the trip and poor Saint Anna is trying her best to avoid being seduced by the sexy Kaidan. She rents one room for both of them, stalks him, kisses him, sees him buck naked the morning after. Next thing you know she’ll be wiggling her ass in front of him and will wonder <i>”Am I giving the wrong signal?”</i>. Well pumpkin it depends on what kind of signal you’re referring to. You’re currently stuck on the <i>bang me</i> one.<br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380373466ra/727088.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Oh dear lord the cheesiness! It feeds on your brain cells like a drunken leprechaun feeds on four leaf clovers.<br><br><br><u>
  <b>A short conclusion?</b>
</u><br>Saint Anna is a fucking idiot, she tries her best to act smart but she fails miserably. Kaidan is the hottest guy on the planet and we keep on getting reminders of that on every page of the book. Patti is the most retarded parent you could ever meet. Predictable. Bullshit. Idiotic. Cheesy. Unoriginal. Boring. Dropped.</span>
  <a data-text-id="2187264620290126056" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_181564291" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/181564291" />
    <a title="FreakChiq" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3530772-freakchiq"><img alt="FreakChiq" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1296820868p2/3530772.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/181564291?book_show_action=true">Jul 03, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="FreakChiq" class="user" itemprop="url" name="FreakChiq" href="/user/show/3530772-freakchiq">FreakChiq</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/13097220-sweet-evil">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3530772-freakchiq?shelf=2012-release">2012-release</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer181564291" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6924546410266487141"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380352504i/705957.jpg' width='279' height='192' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>Yes, <i>Sweet Evil</i> does put an original spin on all the angel/demons/nephilim stories that are out there. But nevertheless, this does not alter the fact that it’s still complete and utter rubbish. The sheer amount of ridiculousness in this 464 pages long novel is dumbfounding. I spent a great deal of time laughing in disbelief or growling in frustration because of it. <br/><br/>The characters are as one dimensional as a stick figure. Their behavior is odd (I don’t know of a single person who talks and acts l</span>
  <span id="freeText6924546410266487141" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380352504i/705957.jpg" width="279" height="192" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Yes, <i>Sweet Evil</i> does put an original spin on all the angel/demons/nephilim stories that are out there. But nevertheless, this does not alter the fact that it’s still complete and utter rubbish. The sheer amount of ridiculousness in this 464 pages long novel is dumbfounding. I spent a great deal of time laughing in disbelief or growling in frustration because of it. <br><br>The characters are as one dimensional as a stick figure. Their behavior is odd (I don’t know of a single person who talks and acts like these characters do), OOC and illogical. And sometimes even just plain wrong.<br><br>Anna is the mother of goodie-two-shoes. She doesn’t lie. (Well, she did once... On purpose. Shocker! Wait till you read what she lied about. LOL. *rolls eyes*) Words like sexy and hott—yes, with a double t—didn’t exist in her vocabulary until she met Kaidan. She cries all the time. She’s naïve. She says one thing, but does the other. She goes all ‘Double Rainbow’ over seeing a rainbow and crossing the state border. The only thing I couldn’t figure out about her—and what drove me a bit crazy—is why the hell she doesn’t own a cell phone.<br><br>Her adoptive mother, Patti, is the worst and most awkward parent ever. Not only did she knowingly allow her just-turned 16-year-old (and extremely naïve) daughter on a 5-day cross-country trip with a 17-yeard-old boy that she doesn’t know at all (and I mean AT ALL), oh no, she also went down the awkward route and told that same boy to bring her daughter back with her <i>virtue intact.</i><br><blockquote>“Hands <i>off,</i> Mister!”</blockquote> Yes, she actually said that. Who talks like this? And what adult weeps like a 10-year-old when facing a problem?<br><br>Anna’s father is the Duke of drinking and drug abuse. He and his demon minions are responsible for all the drunks and drug addicts in this world, basically. So, being the good father that he is, he shows his daughter how to hold her liquor. <br><blockquote>
  <i>“You’re gonna need to learn your drinking limits. I don’t want you to end up in a situation where you don’t know your boundaries.”<br>“How am I supposed to learn?”<br>“You drink. Under my supervision. Well figure out how much you can handle in a certain amount of time, and practice controlling it so you can stay coherent and not get drunk.”</i>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380352504ra/705958.gif" width="265" height="199" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I know she’s supposed to lure people into drinking and stuff, but there are things/words no father, demon or not, should teach/say to his child. <br><br>And then there’s Kaidan. Or as Anna once said: <i>“Kai, like Thai, only yummier.”</i> (*rolls eyes*) He is in a band, he has the looks, an English accent and is the son of the Duke of Lust—totally swoon-worthy bad boy material, right? No. Nope. Absolutely not. A tortured, brooding and fairly boring man-slut/male prostitute, that’s the best and only way to describe Kai. I was utterly disgusted every time he said to Anna that he needs to go ‘working.’ How can you fall for someone who needs to, yes, needs to, fuck some bimbo’s brains out every night is beyond my understanding. <br><br>Just like the characters, the story did, too, rub me totally the wrong way. Higgins completely failed to create a believable and internally consistent narrative. It went from one ridiculous and odd thing to another. The way she moved the story from point A to point B was unsettling. It gave me the feeling that she didn’t care at all how strange and downright bizzare certain things would sound or look like. As if all that she wanted was to get the characters/storylines into a desired position as quickly as possible. Screw logic and common sense.<br><br><b>»</b> No money for a road trip? Let the loaded 17-year-old boy, the MC and her mother just met, offer them both a ride.<br><br><b>»</b> A road trip with a parent would be boring and the parent would endanger the opportunity for long lustful nights? Just write down that the mother has to work. No reader will mind that her child is only sixteen. She will totally come off as a hip and cool mom.<br> <br><b>»</b> But where will they sleep? They can’t rent a room in a motel. Duh, just make Kaidan an emancipated minor.<br><br><b>»</b> It’s time to bring daddy into the picture, but he’s in prison and you really need him out of there? How convenient that he happens to have a parole hearing coming up. That's just so dandy!<br>I could go on and on...<br><br>And don’t even let me start how pointless the whole road trip was in the end.<br><br>Would I recommend this read? No, absolutely not. Not even to my biggest enemy. But seeing how many other readers were thrilled by this book... I don't know. Maybe some of you will, for some inexplicable reason, actually like it. But <i>Sweet Evil</i> <b>most definitely</b> wasn't my cup of tea.</span>
  <a data-text-id="6924546410266487141" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_189492299" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/189492299" />
    <a title="Ezmirelda" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3800177-ezmirelda"><img alt="Ezmirelda" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1358131158p2/3800177.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/189492299?book_show_action=true">Jul 25, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ezmirelda" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ezmirelda" href="/user/show/3800177-ezmirelda">Ezmirelda</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3800177-ezmirelda?shelf=5-stars">5-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3800177-ezmirelda?shelf=must-read">must-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3800177-ezmirelda?shelf=angels">angels</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3800177-ezmirelda?shelf=demons">demons</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3800177-ezmirelda?shelf=the-creme-de-la-creme">the-creme-de-la-creme</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer189492299" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14755317824032082243"> I'm going to be upfront with you about this book—Sweet Evil tops the books coming out in 2012 easily. There's no way I can tell you how much I utterly adore this book, which is why I took me forever to write a proper review for it. I'll start off with why I love this book so much. Originality—finally someone who gets it right! Among all the books out there about angels and demons Sweet Evil has the most original take on them that I've read. The whole badge concept and the fact that the Nephilim</span>
  <span id="freeText14755317824032082243" style="display:none"> I'm going to be upfront with you about this book—Sweet Evil tops the books coming out in 2012 easily. There's no way I can tell you how much I utterly adore this book, which is why I took me forever to write a proper review for it. I'll start off with why I love this book so much. Originality—finally someone who gets it right! Among all the books out there about angels and demons Sweet Evil has the most original take on them that I've read. The whole badge concept and the fact that the Nephilim's sole purpose is being bad influences to humans is pure genius!<br /><br /> The characters. If there's any YA character that is swoon-worthy than Kaidan Rowe is exactly that. Every time he's in a scene of the book I'm practically bouncing up and down with excitement. There isn't a thing I don't like about him. Kaidan is my man. ;) Anna is an amazing female protagonist, and I felt even the side characters were all very well developed. The plot's pacing is perfect. I never felt bored anywhere or felt the need to stop. There was always something interesting to keep my attention. Which brings me to my 3rd reason for loving this—high stakes. The higher the stakes are in a book the more I want to read it. Sweet Evil does not fail in making that happen.<br /><br /> I am completely enamored with SweetEvil. It's one of those books you're only expecting to read for about a half hour or so (because you're busy and have other work you should probably be attending to) and end up reading the whole thing in one sitting, forgetting all the things you had to do that day (Spoken from true experience!). So yeah, even though I've already read this I'm going straight to the bookstore in May to get a shiny brand new copy and will probably re-read it several times until the next one comes out. :)<br /><br /><br />You can also see this review on my blog <a href="http://parafantasy.blogspot.com/2012/02/sweet-evil-by-wendy-higgins-review.html" rel="nofollow noopener">PARAFANTASY</a>. <br /><br /><br />- - - <br /><br />EXTRA THOUGHTS on the whole cross country road trip, her mother shouldn't have allowed her to go, etc stuff that I've seen here:<br /><br />OKAY. So if you have read through the entire novel you know that Patti (Anna's mom) knew that Anna was never going to be just a normal person. She knows that Anna is destined for something. NOW Patti is one of those really (and I mean REALLY) religious people, where if she knew that God wanted her to do something she would do it. Now you can't say parents like this don't exist in the REAL world because they most certainly do. She knows that Anna going on the CROSS-COUNTRY TRIP has a great deal to do with her mission, that if she didn't complete it in time that it wouldn't be working well in God's favor. I'm not much of a religious person but I knew a lot of the things in this book was referenced from biblical text. <br /><br />That is why it makes sense to me that PATTI would allow Anna to go on the trip. If you read the scene about Anna's birth and how Patti came to adopt her it makes sense why Patti would believe that letting Anna go was the right thing for her to do. NOW, if I didn't know any backstory on Anna's birth and wasn't paying attention to her mother's attitude toward religion then I would have thought her consenting to the trip was a crazy idea but that is not the case here. :/</span>
  <a data-text-id="14755317824032082243" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Sana" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/26402455-sana"><img alt="Sana" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1560612398p2/26402455.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1680130157?book_show_action=true">Feb 11, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sana" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sana" href="/user/show/26402455-sana">Sana</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26402455-sana?shelf=boring-af">boring-af</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26402455-sana?shelf=sick-of-this-bitch">sick-of-this-bitch</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1680130157" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10772449909770393611"><b>Yo, listen up, this is a roast/rant review and there's going to be a fuckload of F bombs. You've been warned. And if you liked this book then don't read my review bc you're going to end up pissed off??</b><br/><br/>Guys, never in my life, have I <i>ever</i> something as shitty, annoying and fucking petty as this fucking book. This book made me want to cut my fucking eyeballs out and cry in annoyance and frustration. Never have I read a book <i>this horrible</i>, that I was to the point where it physically hurt me to turn a</span>
  <span id="freeText10772449909770393611" style="display:none"><b>Yo, listen up, this is a roast/rant review and there's going to be a fuckload of F bombs. You've been warned. And if you liked this book then don't read my review bc you're going to end up pissed off??</b><br /><br />Guys, never in my life, have I <i>ever</i> something as shitty, annoying and fucking petty as this fucking book. This book made me want to cut my fucking eyeballs out and cry in annoyance and frustration. Never have I read a book <i>this horrible</i>, that I was to the point where it physically hurt me to turn another page and read the bullshit that is <i>this book</i>. Literally, I am crying tears of pain.<br /><br />First of fucking all, <br />who the fuck let this get published in the fucking <b>Young Adult</b> genre? I'm sorry, who the fuck let this book get <i><b>published</b> at all???</i> And that cover. <b>That fucking cover</b> is so horrible my eyes hurt looking at it. <br /><br /><b>The writing:</b><br />Hey y'all, are you guys <i>sure</i> an <b>adult</b> wrote this??? You sure it's isn't some 12 or thirteen year old? Y'all sure? For real? <b>"W O W Z A"</b> that's a surprise! Literally, what the fucking fuck is the writing. So fucking immature, beyond <b>fucking annoying</b>, bland as fuck, petty as fuck, and did I mention <i>annoying as fucking fuck?</i><br /><br />This is how the author described some of the "things" in this book:<br /><br /><i>
  <b>"My eye glided to the cloud <u>thing</u>, which moved around her..."<br /><br />"The shadow <u>thing</u> floated along next to her..." </b>
</i><br /><br /><b>W O W Z A</b> what a way to fucking describe something 10/10 description you fucking go!<br /><br />The author also gives this shitload of info dumping and i'm just like????? back up???? what the fuck is happening???? like<i>?????</i><br /><br />That's literally nothing, this entire book was me having to read about a fucking whiny special snowflake who couldn't shut the fucking hell up about how much she fucking want Kaidan fucking Rowe. Like, bitch, <b>shut your mother fucking annoying, whiny bitch ass mouth about how fucking hot Kaidan is and how much you want his fucking dick buried in your fucking vagina</b>. I legit feel like this entire book was about this annoying, whiny bitch wanting Kaidan's dick in her vagina, which she sadly mistakes for "love."<br /><br />This fucking Anna girl is so fucking naive and stupid, God help her fucking pathetic ass. I fucking hated her and I'm hoping she dies sometime in the next books. <br /><br />And Kaidan. <b>Mother fucking Kaidan</b> you guys! The hottest guy to ever place foot on the entire fucking earth. Makes every girl panties drip, you guys! He's so fucking hot and Anna couldn't seem to <b>shut the fuck</b> up about how fucking hot he was! BITCH SHUT THE FUCK UP, I GET IT, JESUS FUCKING CHRIST I GET IT HE'S THE SEXIEST PIECE OF MEAT ALIVE, YOU <b>DO NOT</b> NEED TO REPEAT THAT SHIT OVER AND OVER. <br /><br />This entire book is Anna lusting after this bitch Kaidan. I hate Kaidan. And I hope he dies sometime later in the series too! :)<br /><br />P.S the W O W Z A was annoying right? Well it was from the book.... :)<br /><br />BR numero dos with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/45136398-zain-otoom" rel="nofollow noopener">my ass whipper</a> who I couldn't have survived without.</span>

<div id="review_356632021" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/356632021" />
    <a title="Lucia" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8837962-lucia"><img alt="Lucia" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1484242793p2/8837962.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/356632021?book_show_action=true">Jun 27, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lucia" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lucia" href="/user/show/8837962-lucia">Lucia</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/13097220-sweet-evil">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">To all YA paranormal readers</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8837962-lucia?shelf=ya">ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8837962-lucia?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer356632021" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13903104633089669624">My Anna and Kaiden:<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393775060i/8761585._SX540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>“...but even the devout have weaknesses. The demons have to take different measures with different cultures, because some are more accepting of sin, while others are stricter. It’s all a matter of semantics and presentation. They come up with ingenious ways to promote pain and apathy, kind of like marketing schemes. Seek pleasure. Eat, drink, and be merry. Carpe diem.”</b>
</blockquote><br/>Anna is ideal student and equivalent of a good girl. She never lies, because even small harmless lie makes</span>
  <span id="freeText13903104633089669624" style="display:none">My Anna and Kaiden:<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393775060i/8761585._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>“...but even the devout have weaknesses. The demons have to take different measures with different cultures, because some are more accepting of sin, while others are stricter. It’s all a matter of semantics and presentation. They come up with ingenious ways to promote pain and apathy, kind of like marketing schemes. Seek pleasure. Eat, drink, and be merry. Carpe diem.”</b>
</blockquote><br>Anna is ideal student and equivalent of a good girl. She never lies, because even small harmless lie makes her uncomfortable. She is strongly tempted to all "bad" things, but so far she has always been able to resist them. With her extremely enhanced senses and ability to see and feel feelings of other people, she is aware of the fact that she is different. Than she meets attractive drummer and bad boy Kaiden who seems too be different himself and has answers to her questions. The feelings between those two evoke but when Anna discovers her true origin, she realizes that Kaiden may be too bad for her and being together is very dangerous for both of them. Will she be able to resist this sweet evil temptation???<br><br><b>Anna</b> was quite a naive character at the beginning since she was sheltered from all bad her whole life. However, she was extremely nice and compassionate person, she really grew on me and I ended up loving her a lot. <br><br>I really liked <b>Kaiden</b> too. He was destined to do bad things but Anna discovered something good in him, got under his skin and gave him a hope. It was very insteresting to read about how afftected Kaiden was by Anna but simultaneously tried to stay true to his sinful origin. <br><br>Sweet Evil was excellent introduction into this YA paranormal series. I was blown away by <b>angels &amp; demons mythology</b> and original twists in this story. First half was not very action-driven BUT it was very interesting to find out all those information about Nephilims and get to know characters. Moreover, banters and conversations between Anna and Kaiden were entertaining and chemistry between them was off the charts. I was pleasantly surprised that even though Sweet Evil is YA story, some scenes were really hot! The second half was undownputtable, I loved every second of it and I cannot wait to find out what is in store for Anna, Kaiden and other characters in next instalment!<br><br>MORE REVIEWS ON MY BLOG <a href="http://readingismybreathing.blogspot.cz/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <b>Reading Is My Breathing</b>
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="13903104633089669624" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_378641909" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/378641909" />
    <a title="Bookish Indulgenges with b00k r3vi3ws" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4556168-bookish-indulgenges-with-b00k-r3vi3ws"><img alt="Bookish Indulgenges with b00k r3vi3ws" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1548687048p2/4556168.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/378641909?book_show_action=true">Jul 27, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Bookish Indulgenges with b00k r3vi3ws" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Bookish Indulgenges with b00k r3vi3ws" href="/user/show/4556168-bookish-indulgenges-with-b00k-r3vi3ws">Bookish Indulgenges with b00k r3vi3ws</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer378641909" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14653912951539878200">Anna Whitt is anything but normal and she knows it. She can see other people’s ‘feelings’ through the colour of their aura. She feels like a freak except when she is with her friend Jason. Jason eats, breathes and lives music and also has taken Anna into his fold. Around the time for her sixteenth birthday, it is through Jason that Anna meets Kaidan – the HOT drummer with no emotions that she can see/feel. Anna realizes that Kaidan is like her and they take a road trip to go and meet Anna’s fath</span>
  <span id="freeText14653912951539878200" style="display:none">Anna Whitt is anything but normal and she knows it. She can see other people’s ‘feelings’ through the colour of their aura. She feels like a freak except when she is with her friend Jason. Jason eats, breathes and lives music and also has taken Anna into his fold. Around the time for her sixteenth birthday, it is through Jason that Anna meets Kaidan – the HOT drummer with no emotions that she can see/feel. Anna realizes that Kaidan is like her and they take a road trip to go and meet Anna’s father and that is when she slowly discovers about her heritage and who she truly is.<br /><br />The characters in this book are really swoon worthy. Anna is a sweet girl who had been kept in the dark for a long time by her adoptive mother. But when she finds out about herself she accepts it immediately as she had always known that something was different about her. However, she is not one of those overthinking sissy female leads who moans about how unfair her life is or over analyze every situation. She is practical and always ready to do what needs to be done. Kaidan on the other hand comes across this ‘brute’ – a rude and arrogant. But his strength and integrity of character is unquestionable. But the character I loved the most was Kopano. His strength of character is what makes him stand out in the story. Unlike other Nephs who give in to their demon father’s wishes, Kopano took the chance to stand up for what he believed. He went against his very own nature to do what was right. I love him for that.<br /><br />I haven’t read about Nephilim before and my reading experience about angels is truly limited. So this book opened a new world of ideas to me – ideas that I truly liked. There were a few moments in the story that seemed like too much of a coincidence or just too convenient or a bit farfetched, still they weren’t anything major. I was able to just think that ‘this is just fiction after all’ and move on. And specifically for that, I would like to give credit to the author’s style of writing. It was so simple yet engrossing that a few bumps along the way did not matter much. Overall, I liked the plot and I am looking forward to the next part in the installment – just hoping there will be bit more action in it.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="14653912951539878200" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1624869482" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1624869482" />
    <a title="Zain Otoom" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/45136398-zain-otoom"><img alt="Zain Otoom" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1598878687p2/45136398.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1624869482?book_show_action=true">Feb 12, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Zain Otoom" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Zain Otoom" href="/user/show/45136398-zain-otoom">Zain Otoom</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1624869482" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11959480350467168104">So, I'm not going to make a hateful rant where I just stomp on this book and throw it in a blazing fire or flush it down the toilet or ... sorry I got off track. Because, one: many of my friends loved this book; and hey, that's awesome! I wish I did too! Two: I actually was enjoying the first two hundred-ish pages. <br/><b>*Note after writing the review: I know I said I'm not writing a hateful rant but I did get a bit hateful on the characters, just a heads-up!*</b><br/>I did think it was ridiculous, but I was e</span>
  <span id="freeText11959480350467168104" style="display:none">So, I'm not going to make a hateful rant where I just stomp on this book and throw it in a blazing fire or flush it down the toilet or ... sorry I got off track. Because, one: many of my friends loved this book; and hey, that's awesome! I wish I did too! Two: I actually was enjoying the first two hundred-ish pages. <br /><b>*Note after writing the review: I know I said I'm not writing a hateful rant but I did get a bit hateful on the characters, just a heads-up!*</b><br />I did think it was ridiculous, but I was enjoying my time nonetheless! But then it got boring because of all the angst that was thrown at me. Like I didn't sign up for this much drama and oh-he-doesn't-love-me-I'm-nothing-without-him-wah-wah-wah shit, okay?? <br />All I wanted was just a fun easy book to read and forgive all the tiny—huge in this case—problematic troops and cliche romance that can get quite cringe-y. <br />So, Anna, the main sweet virgin who knows nothing about boys and is shy and can't handle herself around other people. Her best and only friend, Jay—because fuck female friends right? They're bitches anyway, except for Anna of course! She a virgin duh! She ain't hanging with all those sluts who only want to sleep with every hot guy they meet, like, duh!! Sorry I got off track again. <br />As I was saying, Jay has to babysit her everywhere, because without him, she might get drugged, raped, killed, or all of them together. She can't read people for shit. <br />Everyone's nice right? They won't hurt me!!!!!!!!!!!!<br />She doesn't say that but that's how her actions translate for me. <br />Kaiden, he was okay in the beginning, kinda jerk face, but who am I to talk, apparently jerks are the hot stuff nowadays. They get all them ladies' panties wet yo. *rolls eyes*<br />Then he has this weird shift in the middle of the book, like who are you??? <br />Now, it got boring for me because of this problem that arose, I was like, "Wait this problem has always existed, since the beginning, why is it only being acknowledged now?" <br />I mean I wish it was like the addicting kind of angst; it was just Anna whining about Kaiden, blah blah blah. FOR. THREE. FUCKING. MONTHS. <br />As I said the problem was there from the beginning!! This whole book wouldn't exist if it was handled at the start!<br />The world is kinda interesting, I admit, but the way the author built it was the worst kind of way. Yes, yes and yes. The hideous info dump. A whole fucking long ass chapter would be Anna talking to someone to help her understand the shit that's happening. SO. BORING. <br />Like seriously, the author couldn't think of another way? I understand that Anna needs someone to tell her the stuff, but really???<br />Anyway. I think 1.5 stars rounded up to two is a fair rating. Not gonna continue on the trilogy because when I think about reading more about Anna and her whining, and how she loves Kaiden and can't move on from him to another dude; I think I'd have more fun watching paint dry. <br /> <br />*****<br />I have been playing DMC on my PC for a while now and it has gotten me into some demon-on-angel-action mood, so yeah, this was my pick. Seems like some ridiculous read, but nonetheless, fun. <br />Another BR with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/26402455-sana-khalid" rel="nofollow noopener">The Devil who like to call me The Ass Whipper</a> . It's not like what you might be thinking, I swear.</span>

<div id="review_613370597" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/613370597" />
    <a title="• Lisa •" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11963959-lisa"><img alt="• Lisa •" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1576172089p2/11963959.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/613370597?book_show_action=true">May 12, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="• Lisa •" class="user" itemprop="url" name="• Lisa •" href="/user/show/11963959-lisa">• Lisa •</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer613370597" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10297275128095320186"><b>THREE I LOVE KAIDAN STARS.</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393684425i/8752042._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='500' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>First things first, this book may have a healthy helping of the sweet but it certainly delivered the evil with that cliff hanger ending. I need to get my hands all over book two in this series and luckily for me it's available to instant one-click. What a likeable, interesting and addictive young adult read. Wendy Higgins is an author who had a tale to tell and has shared it well. Packed to the brim with action, self discovery and a simmering attraction between good and</span>
  <span id="freeText10297275128095320186" style="display:none"><b>THREE I LOVE KAIDAN STARS.</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393684425i/8752042._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>First things first, this book may have a healthy helping of the sweet but it certainly delivered the evil with that cliff hanger ending. I need to get my hands all over book two in this series and luckily for me it's available to instant one-click. What a likeable, interesting and addictive young adult read. Wendy Higgins is an author who had a tale to tell and has shared it well. Packed to the brim with action, self discovery and a simmering attraction between good and evil I think I've found myself an enjoyable paranormal series to get lost in. Read on for my sweet and oh-so-evil book thoughts ...<br><br><b>What's it all about?</b><br>Anna Whitt has always know she was different, growing up with an ability to see and feel the emotions of those around her, she is aware that she has an extraordinary gift. What she's about to discover is that there's a whole world unknown to her that whether she likes it or not she is apart of. During this journey of self discovery she meets the dangerously attractive drummer, Kaidan Rowe, he's the one temptation that she is finding hard to resist, and is discovering that all she wants is to jump into this simmering attraction with abandon. But Anna has much more to discover than just her first love she has a life time of questions and unanswered pieces to the puzzle to unravel and so Anna starts on the path towards finding love, discovering the meaning of her life and fulfilling her destiny. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393684425i/8752043._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>What did I like?</b><br>What a wickedly delicious tale of good vs evil, Wendy Higgins has created a good balance of storyline, fun and young adult appropriate romance. There was plenty to like about this novel and after being on my 'to be read' shelf for longer than necessary I finally decided to take the plunge and although this book didn't sweep me away into 'five-star-love-struck-book-heaven' it certainly gave me a solid enjoyment level of entertainment. The unexpectedness of the story line was the winning factor for this book, the twists and turns and character development all pulled together to make an exiting and interesting race to the finish. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393684425i/8752044._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Why not five?</b><br>Let me start by saying that a three star rating from me means that I enjoyed it, it was likeable, I never wanted to stop reading the book. But when I compared it to what I wold consider 'like-for -like' in this genre it didn't quite meet up to the enjoyment factor of those books or series. One of the main factors for a lesser rating was the lack of butterfly inducing scenes, I missed the character connection somewhat, but having said that this book has got me hooked and I'm more than willing to carry on with the series. My other issue was how close to the bone it felt in terms of spiritual happenings, I think because of my personal faith it might have developed in my mind as too true to likeness of reality, instead of a paranormal romance that is up there with the reality of fairies and goblins. however overall it has an undeniable like-ability factor to it that I'm sure I won't forget about.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393284757i/8687596._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="450" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Final thoughts ...</b><br>This is a young adult paranormal series that has got it's claws in me, I can't wait to pick up book two in this series and I'll be sure to look out for more from this author. One more thing worth mentioning, for a young adult series the characters, Kaidan and Anna were something special I can't wait to learn more about them and hopefully fall in love right along side them. Go grab it readers, I believe book three in the trilogy is available in April. Enjoy ... Kisses.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393684425i/8752045._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>*Buddy read with the bezzie, love my Anna Champion.*</i>
</b></span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

  <a href='http://www.gifbin.com/981354' rel='nofollow noopener'>

<br/><br/>I love Kaidan's POV. I hope that there will be more shorts on his POV. :)<br/>How can I have just read this now? Thank you Pang for letting me know about these shorts!<br/><br/><br/><br/>Merged review:<br/><br/><i> “What are you going to do?”<br/>“Nothing that would compromise your virtue and have Patti hunting me down.”</i><br/><br/>----------------------------------------------------<br/>If an angel and t</span>
  <span id="freeText2870378271337980548" style="display:none"><b>Oh my GOODNESS!</b><br>Seriously Ms. Wiggins I don't know how you do it but you made my legs like jelly again!<br><s>I WANT TO RIP YOUR CLOTHES OFF KAIDAN!</s><br><br>
  <a href="http://www.gifbin.com/981354" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380399543ra/773275.gif" alt="funny gifs" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
<br><br>I love Kaidan's POV. I hope that there will be more shorts on his POV. :)<br>How can I have just read this now? Thank you Pang for letting me know about these shorts!<br><br><br><br>Merged review:<br><br><i> “What are you going to do?”<br>“Nothing that would compromise your virtue and have Patti hunting me down.”</i><br><br>----------------------------------------------------<br>If an angel and the devil were to fall in love, can their love transcend the laws of heaven and hell? Will he set her wings on fire?<br><br>Anna was good.<br>She good in a way that she doesn’t commit any wrongdoing if she could help it.<br>She always had the urge to do the right thing.<br>She wasn’t normal and she knew that all too well.<br>She tried her best to blur out the weird things that were happening to her so that she could live as normally as she could.<br>She was not expecting her world to turn upside down when she met the drummer of the band Lascivious, Kaidan Rowe.<br>Kaidan Rowe was bad news and she knew it.<br>She kept on telling herself it was better to stay away but she couldn’t.<br>There was something about the elusive Kaidan that draws Anna to him.<br>Was it just his charm?<br>They were nothing like each other.<br>But are they really different or more the same?<br><br><b>FIRST IMPRESSIONS</b><br><br>Honestly, the thing that drew me to this book in the first place was the cover and the title.<br>They were pretty good.<br>Sweet evil.<br>You have to admit that title would make you curious.<br>The cover was pretty haunting.<br>The balance of the white and the black and the red gown.<br>It was just so good.<br>But of course I am not very happy with the guy on the cover. <br>He looks like a zombie and Kaidan was NOTHING like that.<br>Kaidan was H.O.T and not C.O.L.D and that guy on the cover was C.O.L.D.<br>Not really Kaidan like for me.<br>I mean I could go on and on all day about Kaidan but I will have to get to that later.<br><br><b>WHAT’S IN IT FOR YOU?</b><br><br>When I started reading this book I was so happy. <br>I loved the writing style and the character Anna already made an impression on me.<br>But then I had to stop for a while because it was too slow for me.<br>I was also seriously thinking about just not finishing the book all together because I am not really a fan of slow paced books. I get bored easily.<br>Still I picked it up and decided to just go on with it and give it another shot.<br>Imagine my surprise!<br>It was so great! I was so glad I finished it.<br>Reading this book gave me a wide range of emotions.<br>It got me serious, happy, sad, scared, curious, anxious, and impatient and a bunch of other stuff.<br>This book is one of those “Let-Me-Surprise-You” books.<br>It will definitely catch you off guard.<br>It will keep you at the edge waiting on what will happen next.<br>I starts out slow then gradually increase pace, then it gets faster and *BBBOOOOMMM*! It will blow your mind!<br>I think the gradual pace change definitely worked for this book.<br>It will give you enough time to adjust with the information that will be shared by the characters about who they are and what they are dealing with.<br>Also another thing that I found good with this book was the use of the angels and the demons.<br>There was some truth in it.<br>I mean we all know what happened to Lucifer and the fallen angels right? And this book stayed true to that but with a bunch of other stuff included.<br>It was pretty believable for me. It almost made me fear that there were such things as the Dukes of Hell and their sons or daughters that roam with us every day without us ever knowing.<br>I am a big fan on angel books and for those who know me, I am a very big fan of the Mortal Instruments and if you are too then you will probably get culture shock when you read this.<br>The use of the Nephilims here are different as to how they were used in the MI or ID.<br>There were a lot of seriously good stuff here.<br><br><b>CHARACTERS</b><br><br><b> Anna</b><br>She was a very fun character to read.<br>I have never once thought I’d enjoy reading about a goody-goody character like her.<br>I was expecting her to be whiny but she wasn’t.<br>She had a lot of self control but *beeeeeeeppppppppp*. I can’t really say because that’s gonna be a major spoiler. You have to read it so that you’ll know!<br>I don’t have any problems with her at all.<br>She also leaves good lines once in a while.<br>She despite being *beeeeeeeeppppp* still has hormones, raging hormones. Hahaha.<br>And although she was good (in every sense of the word), she was still human.<br>She gets hurt. She feels pain. She feels insecure.<br>She was so real to me and I loved that about her.<br>She was flawed and not the perfect but helpless girl in almost every YA books now a days.<br><br><b>Kaidan</b><br><br>I totally take back what I said about not being able to connect with him because I totally could now.<br>I mean wow! This guy had a lot of things going on.	<br>First off, I would like to warn everyone that this guy is oozing with H.O.T.N.E.S.S you’ll feel it through the pages of the book<br>He makes me go like this:<br><br><a href="http://photobucket.com/images/funny%20gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380363385ra/714706.gif" alt="Funny gif Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I know it looks weird but he makes me lick my lips. A lot! Hahaha.<br>He was not your typical lead male character.<br>He wasn’t good. He was H.O.T yes but he was bad news!<br>Yep! This guy is not good news so it’s better to stay away but this guy will make sure you don’t get enough of him because he’s *bbbeeeeeeeeeeeeppp*. (a major spoiler there!)<br>Despite this guy’s sins you’ll still love him because you’ll know he’s not all wicked inside.<br>I just wish Kaidan finds himself or finds me at least. Hahaha. :D<br>I imagine him looking something like this:<br><br><a href="http://photobucket.com/images/ian%20somerhalder%20gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380363385ra/714707.gif" alt="Smiiiiirk Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="http://photobucket.com/images/ian%20somerhalder%20gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <span>[image error]</span>
</a><br><br>If ever this becomes a movie I want him to look somewhat like Ian.<br><br><a href="http://photobucket.com/images/ian%20somerhalder%20gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380363385ra/714709.gif" alt="ian somerhalder gif Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a>	<br><br><b>Other Characters</b><br><br>There are a lot of other characters you should look out for. There’s Anna’s adopted mom Patti who I love to death and Anna’s biological dad who surprised the heck out of me.<br>Jay who has been Anna’s friend from the start was also a cool friend who was clueless on what was going on.<br>At one point of the book you’ll meet Kaidan’s dad, his friends and you’ll be introduced to the life that Kaidan has and what Anna was supposed to have had.<br>Characters were pretty 3 dimensional so they’re pretty good.<br><br><b> KAIDAN + ANNA =</b><br><br>Sure we all want a good story but what’s a good story without a little bit of romance on the side huh?<br><br>Chemistry? Definitely there although at first I thought Kaidan was pretty dull to me but as the story progressed I was like “Boy was I so wrong!”<br>You’ll think Good Anna and Bad Kaidan won’t work? <br>Well I am going to tell you that you are soooo wrong!<br>Just by reading about these two kids make my insides tingle with excitement.<br>I was so under their spell. I was just speechless although out<br><br><a href="http://photobucket.com/images/ian%20somerhalder%20gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380363385ra/714710.gif" alt="ian somerhalder gif Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>It was this steamy! Hahaha. Just kidding.<br>This book was steamy but not that graphic or anything. I won’t recommend it to younger kids though.<br>But really Anna and Kaidan? They are just so perfect for each other. Like it or not but they are.<br><br><b>Closing Thoughts</b><br><br>This book was such a surprise to me. I never expected myself to really like it and devour it and get addicted to it like this. There is just so much to love about this book. One of which is the flow of the story slow but gradually increasing until you throw yourself out of your seat because of excitement. One thing I didn’t exactly like was the ending. I just HATE CLIFFHAGERS! But still I adore it all the more because it kept me interested enough to know what will happen to this steamy uncanny couple. Give me the next book already Wendy! I want to get more Kaidan!<br><br>Wendy I want to hug you and never let you go for making such a successful and greatly addictive read. I am definitely a fan! So excited for the next book!<br><br><a href="http://photobucket.com/images/excited%20gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380363385ra/714711.gif" alt="excited gif Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="http://photobucket.com/images/excited%20gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380363385ra/714712.gif" alt="excited gif Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>A perfect 5!</b></span>

    <a title="Danny" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3254909-danny"><img alt="Danny" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1301556302p2/3254909.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/246478580?book_show_action=true">Dec 13, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Danny" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Danny" href="/user/show/3254909-danny">Danny</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3254909-danny?shelf=imm-april12">imm-april12</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer246478580" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12811252800513030980"><a href='http://bewitchedbookworms.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'> Review posted at Bewitched Bookworms</a><br/><br/>You know why I love reading? It’s because of books like this! This book seriously blew me away with it’s epic awesomness! Remember last week when I was raving and fangirling over Of Poseidon? Be aware, this will happen again, right now!<br/><br/>*takes a deep breath*<br/><br/><b>A Tale of Goodness and Evil, packed with an Epic Love Story</b><br/>Sweet Evil is a story about evil and an epic forbidden love story! Anna was always able to see the aura of other people and she knew she was differ</span>
  <span id="freeText12811252800513030980" style="display:none"><a href="http://bewitchedbookworms.com/" rel="nofollow noopener"> Review posted at Bewitched Bookworms</a><br /><br />You know why I love reading? It’s because of books like this! This book seriously blew me away with it’s epic awesomness! Remember last week when I was raving and fangirling over Of Poseidon? Be aware, this will happen again, right now!<br /><br />*takes a deep breath*<br /><br /><b>A Tale of Goodness and Evil, packed with an Epic Love Story</b><br />Sweet Evil is a story about evil and an epic forbidden love story! Anna was always able to see the aura of other people and she knew she was different, yet she never knew why. It’s when she meets Kaidan … *pause*… that she begins to discover who and what she is. And… its not pretty!, it’s terrifying and shatters Anna’s world!<br /><br />The whole story was fast paced, never boring and I especially loved the time frame. This first book spans around 8 month of Anna’s Life and it gives so much room for development which is what I especially loved! There is so much happening, yet never overwhelming. (Although, I was admittedly and constantly overwhelmed by Kaidan’s presence..)<br /><br /><b>Anna – sweet adorable innocent Anna!</b><br />Anna was such an incredible wonderful character and I wanted to hug her simply for being her. She’s the sweetest and nicest girl you can imagine, there is nothing considerably bad about her. You might say this sounds boring and stereotype much, yet it is simply Anna’s nature to be so sweet. It’s pure her and it feels utterly genuine and real. I loved Anna with her naivety and innocence and she as a character worked absolutely perfect for this story!! Anna never felt wrong to me and it’s due to Wendy Higgins talent that I fell in love with this adorable girl!<br /><br /> <br /><br /><b>*fans self* Kaidan … *dies* </b><br />Kaidan .. *pauses* is the perfect and exact opposite to Anna. He’s alluring, mysterious, thrilling and he is seductive. (*oh my… he’s Seductive with a Captial S) Oh and I should mention his british accent -*swoons*. He is one of those characters that instantly made an impression and you cannot turn away from him, being utterly fascinated by this boy the instant he enters to the stage! In all honesty, I have no words to describe the effect Kaidan had on me. He featured everything I love in paranormal novels including his outrageous attitude, seductive hotness, strong package and the promise that there is more inside him which needs to be discovered.<br /><br />In Kaidan, there is no innocence, he’s the bad boys girl fall for and get broken. He uses girls, throws them away, yet he mostly comes out unscathed. Anna is the first girl who is not falling for his charm instantly – she’s simply not the girl who likes to play games. At the same time, Anna is the first girl that ever wants to look into his soul and his heart – something incredibly frightening for Kaidan. There is something about Anna that will ruin everything he has ever believed in …<br /><br /><blockquote>He was smoking hot. As in H-O-T-T, hott. I’d never understood until that moment why girls insisted on adding an extra t. This guy was extra-t-worthy. – Anna, Sweet Evil, ARC pg.10</blockquote><br /><br /><blockquote>Good gracious, he was sexy – a word that had no existed in my personal vocabulary until now. - Anna, Sweet Evil, ARC, pg. 18</blockquote><br /><br /><b>Love, steamy Hottness, Heartbreak, Butterflies and Tears… Tears and Tears</b><br />This whole story was incredible emotional and Wendy Higgins has this incredible talent to make you feel what their characters felt. I was right there with Anna, feeling her emotions instead of reading them, absorbing them and making them my own. THIS is why I read, this is what I want! I want to feel the butterflies when they kiss I want to feel the heartbreak and I want to shed tears with them! Sweet evil is all that and more! Moreover, Sweet Evil is incredibly sexy – it’s hot, it’s steamy yet it still stays suitable for an older YA readership. We never get too far, although this teasing was driving me nuts!<br /><br /><br /><br /><b>Bottom Line:</b><br />Sweet Evil by Wendy Higgins is a highly seductive read, with intense and memorable characters which will suck you into their tale and occupy your mind even after finishing the last page. Anna is an adorable heroine perfect for a tale of good and evil and Kaidan is her perfect counterpart who will enter your dreams and won’t let you go! *dies of this epicness*</span>
  <a data-text-id="12811252800513030980" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>
